gpz note: this one is abusing a resource to keep the contents of the eeprom on the ide64 cartridge - there should be no gui items for it (as it should only be changed by the ide64 software itself). it should perhaps get changed to use an image file for the config data instead (as with eg mmcr)
blacky note: I agree with a change to put this in an image, maybe something like an ide64.nvram image, this is because such an image could be saved immediately when changed, instead of relying on a 'save current settings'.
